Touhou 11: Subterranean Animism but they all have sex instead

by iwant2fuckevery2hugirl

Summary

A lewd retelling of Touhou 11: Subterranean Animism. A hot spring has erupted from the ground, much to the enjoyment of Reimu and Marisa! Unfortunately, spirits from deep within the earth begin shooting out of the geyser. How will they have a hot spring orgy now? Youkai friends lend them powerful magic and send them underground to investigate the disturbance, communicating and peeping at them as they adventure below the earth. Will they discover the secret of the geysers buried deep underground, or will they be too busy burying their dicks inside youkai instead? Who left this fishing rod here?

Chapter 1: Stage 1: Eye Of The Spider

Chapter Summary

Our shine maiden heroine sets off on her adventure into a dark, dank, massive cavern, heading deep underground to find the source of the haunted geysers. On her way, she meets up with her rival and very sexy girlfriend, our magician heroine, who just happens to be on the same quest as her. The duo find out that the descent is fraught with peril, from rockfalls to hungry and needy youkai! Will their partner youkai's borrowed magic powers and big shafts be enough to quell these dangers?

No, because they aren't gonna fuck the boulders. Sorry guys.

As he engrossed himself in the strange game, he sipped at what looked like a can of energy drink from the outside world. And also make people cry by beating them in the multiplayer deathmatch mode and saying she fucked their moms!

This "Yuugi Gmod Smexual Bar Fight Scene" is another one of my ideas for high-effort twist scenes, similar to Alice, Kaguya, Mokou, and Aya's stages. With it done, I gotta admit I'm running out of the ones I initially thought up. I dunno if I will come up with more stuff later, since I came up with a bunch of them for Touhou 6-11 + 15, the games I was most passionate about covering, then haven't had many more ideas for the rest of the series. I might come up with more stuff as I get there, though.

Stage 3 I feel is always a turning point for the plot as it marks the point where the characters stop fucking around and get a lead on the true antagonist. Either this stage or the one after it are the ones where they start to encounter the antagonist's minions, or at least make it to their lair. Therefore I usually try to preserve this aspect when I write these fics. It's a pretty important thing to understand when writing a retelling fanfic, even one about SEX and BOOBS.

Chapter 6: Intermission III: How Halo 3 Saved My Parents' Marriage

Chapter Summary

Sanae has retrieved the package and brought it to her home, the Moriya Shrine. Time to pop this sucker into her Xbox and teabag some (HOMOPHOBIC SLUR OMMITTED)! Intermission III

BGM: Deference for Darkness (from Halo 3: ODST)

By the time Sanae got to the top of Youkai Mountain, silver clouds had rolled overhead and had begun to sprinkle all of Gensokyo with a chilly, wintry rain. It was December, Sanae thought, and by the will of the gods it should at least be snowing. She had learned about global warming in school, and at the back of her mind this winter was her realization that if an alternative to fossil fuels was not found her generation would pay the price. Though, was there even anything a fledgeling god such as herself could do to save the future?

Sanae pushes these doubts to the back of her mind. At the moment there was no use worrying about major issues like global warming and population decline. Nestled behind her arms, shielded from the rain was the game she had sought after for so long. Even if it never snowed again, Halo 3 would definitely have an amazing winter-themed multiplayer level like the first two games that she could play on. Her memories of laying waste to her opponents on Lockout were just as cherished as those where she spent the holidays with her family. Though, the snowy missions in both games that were long, repetitive, and crawling with rocket-launcher toting zombies were much less fondly remembered. She hoped they didn't bring those back...

Last fall Lady Kanako had transported the Moriya Shrine, pillars and all, into Gensokyo atop this mountain claimed by youkai. She had joked to herself that she was a lot like like Master Chief, crash-landing in a glimmering metal spaceship, the Pillar of Autumn, onto the mysterious Halo ring. Just like the man himself, her day-to-day life consisted of dodging past excessive volumes of colorful, glowing bullets and lasers, where even one hit was fatal. Though, unlike him she could fly. Maybe that made things easier? She didn't really have super strength though, or even a hint of his cowboy-like charisma.

In fact, she and her gods were the subject of much suspicion and derision among Gensokyo's inhabitants. The youkai of the mountain were business partners and friends with benefits, but the intimacy ended there. Most considered Sanae to be an incompetent outsider foolishly serving Kanako's whims. She accepted that there were still things for her to learn about Gensokyo even now, but she could do more than hold her own! She just needed to be given a chance to prove herself. Like solving an incident! She couldn't go off to solve anything without Lady Kanako's permission, and Reimu was pretty quick to go off and deal with them on her own. But one day, Sanae hoped, fate would align and she could finally go off on her own journey to fuck youkai and solve an incident.

Even worse, though, were the suspicions revolving around Kanako like orbiting electrons. With the secretive deals she made with the tengu and kappa, and both clans inexplicably growing in strength by the day, there was constant talk of conspiracy. Everyone in Gensokyo had their own theories on secret projects and schemes being cooked up by the deity within her mountain lake enclave. Brainwashing lasers! Tengu cyborgs! Mechas! Solar panel farms! Her secretly wearing a snake-shaped vibrator! A weapon to surpass danmaku! Every theory was more outlandish than the rest, because Gensokyo is full of crazy people. The tengu did not even write about these insane theories out of mutual respect for their business partner. But the absence of such stories alongside their typical inaccurate, lewd reporting, or anything negative or embarassing about the Moriya Shrine at all in itself aroused even more suspicion. Was the snake god censoring the media?

Luckily, Sanae didn't let any of this bother her. Who cares if youkai like that baka ice fairy and her gang were suspicious of her? Most of the youkai still wanted to drain her dry then eat her, at the end of the day, so there was no skin off her back. At least Gensokyo's more sensible inhabitants were a lot friendlier with her, like Rinnosuke and Reimu. She was also quite popular in the Human Village, which was kind of the only thing that mattered. Despite being on top of the mountain the Moriya Shrine was already beating the Hakurei Shrine in popularity by miles. Even more people grabbed her tits and ass and fucked her in the street than they did with Reimu! Hopefully she isn't too mad about that.

Besides, it wasn't time to worry about that. She had just arrived at the Moriya Shrine! It was time to finally play this video game. Sanae lands on her feet in the grounds of the shrine, right in front of the main building. The rain was chasing her, ramping up into an imminent deluge. She shields the disc case from the rain beneath her torso and sprints under the roof of the shrine, the falling rain urging to rush even faster towards safety.

The sliding door to the shrine was open a bit, and bright light filtered through the paper. Two sillhouettes, one tall and one short, were projected onto the surface like a shadow play. Kanako and Suwako must be inside, Sanae supposed. She couldn't wait to tell her moms that she had finally managed to obtain Halo 3! They would be so happy to hear of her wish being granted. Sanae reaches toward the edge of the door...

The sound of someone yelling inside the shrine makes Sanae freeze up, fingers inches from the door. Someone else was yelling back, she realizes. The voices were unmistakable. Were Kanako and Suwako... fighting? Sanae silently peeks inside the shrine through the crack in the door.

"This new scheme of yours will never work. It's risky, it's... suicidal! Just think, Kanako!" Suwako yells, glaring angrily at Kanako from across the main room of the shrine.

"I AM thinking! Thinking of the future! All I want is to keep us and Sanae safe forever. Becoming a patron god of science is the only way to do that. Why can't you just trust me?" Kanako snaps back, shaking her fists with anger.

The two gods stand on opposite sides of the room. Neither of them wanted to be close to the other right now. They both thought it was best to stow away their feelings, protecting them from the venom they would be spitting through the air at eachother. At least, that's what they wanted. The room itself was a mess. Various things were knocked over and strewn about. There were scorch marks all along the walls. From danmaku, no doubt. The walls behind the two gods were spotless, though, and only the perpendicular ones were damaged. It was clear they were just striking out at the building in anger, not hurting eachother. It still hurted Sanae to see them fight like this, even worse than a spell card duel. The two gods' argument continued...

"Sponsoring science? Kanako, this is absurd! Science is the logical enemy of us gods. You can't harvest faith from scientifically minded humans! You're practically ordering your followers to explain us out of existence!"

"You don't know anything! Faith and science have always been able to coexist. Even during the height of our power, humans utilized science without doubting us! They observed the world we granted them and tried to understand how it worked so they could manipulate it to their benefit. Even your own followers used it! How else were they to shape the metal you supplied them into tools and weapons? Cease this useless fearmongering!"

"No, a little bit of science is necessary for any human society to thrive. The craftsman, the farmer, and the wise man all intuit the natural rules of the world as they labor. But you... the science you're sponsoring goes way too far! Nothing good will come of mortals mastering the secret inner workings of the atom. With that knowledge, they'll be able to control reality like the gods! And as gods themselves, they'll see no need for us anymore. Kanako, you've doomed us all!"

Even now, just as before, the mortals depend on miracles from the gods to make these scientific breakthroughs. In exchange for these miracles, they shall give me, their god, faith."

"This logic is utter lunacy! You will kill us all! Think of what will happen to us, to Sanae, when your plan backfires!"

"No, it is a foolproof plan! I, as a god of science, have lifted the holy grail of atomic wisdom from the neverending sea of scientific fantasy and delivered it to the mortals. They shall use this wisdom to produce endless, clean, renewable energy which can be used to improve their lives. In exchange, they will hold reverence for me forever, and followers all over will offer me their faith as thanks for salvation! The more secrets I bestow, the more faith my investments shall return. The world has little use for gods of the wind and earth anymore. Science is the way forward!"

Suwako angrily stomps her feet, making the googly eyes of her big hat roll around in their sockets.

"No! I know you, Kanako! I know what you're like! Your greedy aspirations have always been too strong, for as long as we've known eachother! This is just another conquest for you. Just like my kingdom, just like Gensokyo! When greed seizes your heart, you become a different woman. A monster..."

"No. This time, I'm putting a stop to you. I have to protect you from yourself. I have to... protect Sanae. It's time I finally step up and do what has to be done. Kanako, my love, please don't hate me for this."

Suwako barely suppresses a sob. She makes a gesture from the floor with her hand, then does a rising motion.

"Mishaguji, arise."

At Suwako's command numerous ghostly figures raise out of the ground, phasing through the floor, around her feet. They take the form of misty white snakes, staring Kanako down with glowing red eyes. Immediately, the inside of the Moriya Shrine grows ominously cold, and the lights dim. Kanako looks back at the creatures fearfully, her jaw dropping in shock. Beads of sweat build up on her cheeks. Sanae looks at the creatures fearfully through the doorway, scared into silence. Her fingers grab down tightly onto her disc case, the plastic now feeling warmer than the chilly air engulfing her.

Suwako sticks her hand out, and one of the Mishaguji twists its body around it like a pet. She subconsciously seeked affection from these serpents, yet their adoration did nothing to soothe her heart. She knew what she had to do would not grant her any comfort.

"The Mishaguji? Are you serious, Suwako? Are you really going to use these damned creatures to stop my plan?"

Suwako nods.

"Yes. Using the Mishaguji, I shall curse your plans with misfortune. I'll send them to sabotage that facility you had built and shut down the experiment being run there. You can't stop me. Either submit yourself, or watch helplessly as my assistants destroy your plan. I don't want to hurt you, either way."

You used these things to rule your kingdom with an iron fist, coercing faith from your subjects under threat of misfortune. You even use them to blackmail me, retaining your dominion over our shrine in the shadows while I perform public relations. Is that not the same as me? Do you not claim to be doing whatever you must in order to survive?"

Both of their eyes were red with tears. Neither god wanted to oppose the other. Words could not describe how badly both wanted to give up, embrace the other, and apologize profusely for the hurtful insults they flung at eachother. But this was impossible. Each woman held convictions that were simply too strong to betray, and they both had everyone's wellbeing at heart. They simply disagreed over a single, fundamental point. So out of love, they grew angry at eachother and fought.

This ordeal was painful for Kanako. Her heart beat frantically, quivering on the edge of breaking. Nearly driven to tears, she barely kept herself from crying out loud.

The short goddess was equally devastated. This angry quarrel made her want to die on the spot. But she couldn't even dream of giving up like that. She loved two people very, very much, and it was her duty to protect them. Even if it hurt.

"I don't want to die, Kanako. I don't want any of us to die..."

Kanako can feel the determination in Suwako's eyes, even staring at her through shadows. There was no more negotiating to be done. She steps forward, entering a threatening stance.

"That's it, then. If there's no way to get through to you, then I have no other choice. I'm going to finally kill those damned serpents of yours."

The Mishaguji lash angrily around Suwako, ready to tear the offending god apart. The only thing keeping them in line was Suwako's silence. The earth god stays silent for a moment, before angrily dropping her metal ring to the ground. She speaks to Kanako solemnly.

Suddenly, the front door flies open. There stands Sanae, soaking wet in the rain and streaking tears. She rushes into the middle of the room and stands between the two to stop them from fighting.

"Sanae!" the goddesses exclaim in unison.

"This, humans, is the entrance to the Remains of Blazing Hell. It is the only part of Former Hell that hasn't cooled down. The Yamas ordered the Palace of the Earth Spirits built on top of the entrance to seal it off." Satori explains.

Marisa moves to make a comment, but Satori cuts her off.

"No, just because you beat the Yama before doesn't mean you're able to beat up the entire palace. I don't know what this "powerscaling" thing is, but it sounds stupid."

Marisa pouts, disappointed. Satori continues.

"My pets are tasked with stoking the flames below. If Orin would ever go hide somewhere, she'd go down here. If you see her, please bring her back to me instead of exterminating her! She may be a powerful youkai, but she's also just a cat. She doesn't know any b- Oh, you want to fuck my cat, Reimu."

All three of them go red with embarassment!

"Oh, s-sorry about that, Reimu."

Reimu chuckles from unease.

"No, it's, um, alright... but what does this have to do with the incident?"

"The incident, yes. Orin wasn't the only one of my pets that went missing. I had a pet raven who disappeared without warning, too. I had her tend to the flames as well. If there are geysers full of earth spirits appearing on the surface like you said, I think the Remains of Blazing Hell has to be connected somehow. I'm too weak to investigate myself, but you two seem strong enough to go in my place. Please, you must investigate the Remains of Blazing Hell and find my pets!"

Reimu nods and gives Satori a thumbs-up.

"Of course we will, Satori! We'll find your pets and bring them back to you, then get to the bottom of the geysers. Leave it to me and Marisa! And Yukari, and Alice, and Aya, and Suika, and.."

She gets interrupted by a loud burp from her ying-yang orb.

"Ey! If shit's goin' down back in the remains of old Hell, that's gotta be some wild incident! I never visited the place myself, but my friends said it was hot and chock full o' evil spirits. That's gotta be the cause of the geysers!" Suika exclaims, drunk. "Be careful, Reimu! There's toooons of *wild* shit down there! If our mastermind can make geysers appear above ground from all the way down there, they gotta be, uh, at least half as strong as me!"

Marisa turns to one of her dolls.

"Alice, are ya okay with me bringing these dolls you made into actual, literal, burning Hell, ze?" she asks.

"They should be perfectly safe, Marisa! I only filled them with gunpowder!" Alice answers.

"Aw, hell yeah! I can't wait to get blown up and fucking die, da ze!" Marisa responds, excitedly.

The two give Satori one last nod of thanks and turn to the metal lid. Marisa hops up on top and grabs ahold of the crank.

"Alright, Reimu, I'm gonna open it! You ready, da ze?"

"Sure thing! Marisa, crank that Soulja Boy!"

Inside Marisa's house, the four youkai watch Marisa crank that on the television in silence. Koakuma plays a few fitting notes on a steel drum for Patchouli's entertainment. Besides that, nobody else makes a sound for a while.

Alice suddenly flips the cellphone closed, so that nobody on the other side can hear. She turns around towards the other women, solemnly.

"Okay, about that youkai, we all saw what happened. I think it goes without saying that we should never speak of this ever again. Everyone understand?"

Nitori, Patchy, and Koakuma nod. The librarian deems it a good chance to elaborate things.

"Yes, the satori. A truly pitiable race of creatures. They've been said to have been terrorizing human travelers since ancient times by speaking their thoughts out loud to the world. It makes sense why they would be despised, even by other youkai, but that doesn't make their fate any less tragic. The satori are mostly extinct nowadays. That woman must be one of the last of her kind. Such a shame. That third eye of hers is an amazing gift, even with all its downsides."

"I must admit, as much as I feel bad for her, I'd still prefer to never cross paths with a satori." Alice states. "Especially after seeing one rudely comb through me and Marisa's private memories and say uncouth things about us."

"I doubt we'll ever come across one, even in Gensokyo. That Satori really must've been the last of her kind!" Nitori deduces.

"Yeah!" exclaims the satori in the black hat standing in the corner of the room, though nobody ends up noticing her.

Chapter End Notes

Happy Valentine's Day! I managed to finish this chapter just in time. And for probably the most fitting character, too.

Sorry for the disappearance guys, I decided to take a break to focus on other things in my life for a bit. I'm done, though, and will focus on continuing now. Thanks for all the kind words you guys gave me while I was away. I really do enjoy reading about how much people like this series.

Through my research into mythical satori, I've come across an extremely important nuance regarding Satori's powers that I've never seen anyone in the community acknowledge. It genuinely clears up all the bullshit around our favorite schizo anime sisters. Like, I think I literally unlocked her actual canon personality.

Satori don't just read minds. In particular, they read *the current thoughts of people* and *instantly blurt them out loud*. This makes so much about Satori make a lot more sense. Hating her out of suspicion because she can read minds is cruel, but the real deal is a lot more nuanced than that. Either she impulsively states people's thoughts out loud, or is like that because she is a satori and that is how they act. It isn't stated but the point I'm making is that she states what people are currently thinking out loud.

This ability makes Satori literally unable to properly live in a legitimate society. You can't hold a conversation with her because she will instantly interrupt anyone with the announcement of your inner thoughts. Her mind reading is disruptive, extremely invasive towards others, and possibly can't be controlled. This makes a lot more sense as to why, besides how most youkai seem to be assholes, Satori and Koishi are specifically hated instead of just avoided.

This take also makes Koishi a lot more profound as well. She essentially mutilated a part of herself, shutting down a body part she had just as part of the way she was born, because she couldn't stop it from doing its thing. All because everyone hated her for being so unintentionally disruptive. Yeah this is standard Koishi antics but "shut third eye because people didn't like her mind reading ability" vs "shut third eye because she couldn't stop herself from making everyone angry and being unable to even hold a conversation" is very different.

I don't intend for this to be a statement on canon. I've read Satori's lines ingame and she does indeed speak frequently by stating the protagonist's current thoughts out loud. This is usually interpreted as "oh its so we know she reads minds" but it does fit. Also, the detail that she uses hypnosis to make characters remember the most feared spell cards because she can only read current thoughts actually lines up with this. However I read a bit of her dialogue in CDS and in that manga, she actually doesn't speak people's thoughts out loud. She just reads minds normally. However, CDS is notorious for having absolute fucking garbage writing where ZUN frequently mischaracterizes his own damn characters. It also came out more than a decade after SA, so maybe he forgot? I dunno.

This is a fanwork so I can do this stuff here but I sort of wanted to spread this idea around because I think Satori's neat and hate to see her dismissed as bland. Unfortunately I'm stating this on a porn burner account so in all likelihood it wont reach far.

Also, I took the game screencap myself. I'm not actually good at playing Touhou so I just used practice mode and ended up dying enough times anyway to make it look kinda convincing...

Chapter 8: Intermission IV: they put le sanae in the soder

Chapter Summary

Kanako and Suwako agree to put their conflict on hold and join forces in another one instead: helping Sanae beat Halo 3 on it's infamous highest difficulty! Along their virtual quest to save the galaxy from the eponymous ringworld, they'll learn a thing or two about faith, belief, hope, and noob combos. Time to get really angry at video games!

Chapter Notes

See the end of the chapter for notes

Intermission IV

They let me pick. Did I ever tell you that? Choose whichever Spartan I wanted. You know me. I did my research. Watched as you became the soldier we needed you to be.

Like the others, you were strong and swift and brave. A natural leader. But you had something they didn't. Something no one saw but me. Can you guess?

Mission 1: Arrival

Brace for impact.

BGM: Luck (from "Halo 3")

"Ohhh my gosh! It's actually happening!" Sanae squeals, kicking her feet around excitedly in her frog-adorned pajama bottoms.

The shrine maiden can barely contain her excitement as the beginning of Halo 3 unfolds before her. The game opens with a vista of a starry nighttime sky, crossed by what appeared to be a blazing asteroid descending from space. Inquisitive flutes and the suspenseful stringe of a violin set a mood of cautious optimism in the face of the vast unknown. Etched upon a meager old CRT television screen, the twinkling stars look exactly like the real thing.

"The graphics, they look amazing! It looks exactly like when I fly around Gensokyo at night..." she mutters, struck with awe.

Kanako side-eyes her with concern.

"You mean you fly around at night past your bedtime? Sanae..." she scolds.

"Um, not recently! I swear, I've been a good girl for the past month, Lady Kanako!" Sanae confesses, worriedly.

"You'd better keep being our wonderful, well-behaved daughter, dear. Suwako and I are being very generous letting you stay up this late to play video games. Got it?"

"Yes, Lady Kanako..."

On the screen, a small ball of fire breaks off from the larger one. It descends even faster, zooming in close to them. Seemingly right before the shooting star can fly straight out of the screen, it makes a hard turn and flies above and behind the cutscene's camera. The tips of the leafy trees glow white, and a distant explosion rocks the world of the game. To Sanae and her moms, the boom sounds just like the real thing. Just what was this comet?

"When does the actual video game start?" Suwako interrupts impatiently.

"It's a cutscene, Mom! It's like a short movie part that happens before the playable part starts. It should start for real soon."

"Oh. Ribbit."

The screen cuts to a scene depicting a group of soldiers deep within a jungle. They gather around a deep, smoldering crater with melancholy faces issued as commonly as assault rifles. The camera angle shifts, and the three are presented a view of a limp, still hand clad in green metal armor. The implications make Sanae gasp. She can barely make a sound as the soldiers inspect the center of the crater.

An African-American man smoking a large cigar and wearing a seargent's cap looks over the unmoving body of the massive armored supersoldier. The very next shot shows the Master Chief in his armored entirety, from helmet to boot, laying in the mud like a discarded action figure. The squad corpsman looks over a set of portable scanning equipment and tells the seargant the bad news. The odds of Chief surviving his heavenly aren't particularly comforting.

His face slack with solemn defeat, the seargent kneels down and removes a data chip from a slot in the back of Master Chief's helmet. It was one of the most realistic-looking human facial expressions Sanae had ever seen in a video game. She leans forward on the couch, hooked on the sheer suspense of the scene. Back on the screen, the seargent gives the squad orders in a reverent, reserved tone.

"Radio for VTOL, heavy lift gear. We're not leaving him here."

A hand in green suddenly shoots up and grabs ahold of his wrist.

"Yeah, you're not."

The Chief pulls himself up while holding onto Johnson's wrist. The seargent gasps in relief, but doesn't let up his hardened tone.

"Crazy fool. Why do you always jump?" he asks the Chief sarcastically. "One day, you're gonna land on somethin' as stubborn as you are! And I don't do bits and pieces!"

The helmeted visor of the Chief looks down at the man from an entire foot above him.

"No reason to worry. Lady Kanako always has my back."

Johnson gives him a wry smile.

"So she does. But where's Cortana, Chief?"

He shows Chief the empty data chip that was supposed to hold Cortana. Captain Keyes had given Chief this very same chip seemingly forever ago, shortly before crashing his ship on the first Halo Ring, and it had contained the AI Cortana constantly since. Until now. Chief glances at it silently for a moment, then speaks briefly.

"She stayed behind. With the youkai, at the shrine. Drinking party."

He takes the empty chip and puts it back into his helmet with a faint click. By Lady Kanako's will, Cortana's main process would occupy this chip like a divine spirit once more. After they reunited.

Behind Johnson, Chips Dubbo turns his head and whispers worriedly into Mendoza's ear.

"The hell's the Chief talkin' 'bout? Shroines? Youkai? Ya think he's gotta screw loose, or somethin'?"

"No shit, ese! He probably got messed up bad from that fall, man! I hope the Chief didn't go loco on us."

Johnson overhears them and turns around with an annoyed sneer. He raises his voice at them like they're all back at space marine boot camp.

"Do I hear you wettin' your pants, marines? You gotta have more than a few screws loose like the Chief if you wanna live to see the end of this war! Do I make myself clear, privates?"

Off to the side, Bisenti speaks up.

"Um, ya sure about that, Sarge? I mean, he wasn't talkin' about weird stuff before we found 'im lyin' out here. Sounds to me like his head's stuck in ancient Japan or somethin'!"

Johnson turns around and gets up in Bisenti's face. He can smell the Italianness coming off his skin, even over the choking scent of cigar smoke.

"Weren't you payin' attention in boot camp, marine? All that shit about fairies and ghosts and youkai is one hundred percent, scientifically proven, undoubtedly real! I even met a rabbit livin' on the Moon once! If the Master Chief says that he played Grifball with an oni, you damn better believe he played Grifball with an oni. Do I make myself clear?"

Beads of sweat trickle down the suprised marine's face. Years of training tell him the worst possible thing he can do is get on his seargent's bad side. Him and the rest of the marines decide to resign and go along.

"Y-yes, sir..."

Johnson steps away and blows out a puff of smoke from his cigar. He taps Bisenti on the shoulder.

"You better, boy. When we get back to base in one piece, I'm makin' you, Chips, and Mendoza beat Embodiment of Scarlet Devil without any continues. Now, lets get the hell outta this soup. On the double."

Chief's head jerks toward the bushes behind the group. He notices a faint shimmer in the air emerge from the brush and begin to approach them. He's seen this a million times before, especially across the ironsights of a smoking gun. It materializes into a figure in ornate metal armor, a tall reptilian alien with brown skin and four mandibles in place of a jaw. Moving on pure impulse, Chief grabs Johnson's magnum from his holster and sprints right up to the alien, shoving the gun barrel right into his jaw. He's face-to-face with the Arbiter, current military leader of the Elites and his longtime rival.

Arby freezes up with the Chief's new gun in his mouth. Johnson whirls around and calls out to Chief as the super soldier runs past him.

"Chief, wait! The Arbiter's with us!"

Hearing this, Chief relaxes the finger holding the trigger of the magnum. Arbiter glares back at him angrily. Johnson catches up to him and puts his hand on his shoulder.

"Come on, now! We got enough to worry about without you tryin' to kill eachother!"

At Johnson's behest, the Chief lowers the gun away from the Arbiter's jaws. He looks up at the alien, who was even taller than him, and speaks.

"Sorry. Still used to how they do greetings in Gensokyo. Can't let yourself be held back by common sense."

The Arbiter looks down at him, still angry at the Chief's rudeness. To an Elite like him, such an impulsive gesture was the deepest insult possible, and usually met with certain death. Only a wise Elite such as him would grant the Demon his grace and let it slide. With a chomp of his mandibles, he lets Chief off with a warning.

"Were it so easy."

The hostility between the two was gone, but the tension remained. Arbiter steps away from the Chief and turns away, walking back towards the path through the jungle.

"These humans have put their faith in me in exchange for my holy strength. With the blessing of me and the Elites, the lying Prophets and the rest of their foolish Covenant shall perish screaming in agony beneath searing divine bullets. We must go. The Brutes have our scent."

The Chief, Johnson, and the marines start to follow him. The seargent grins and lets loose another wisecrack.

"Then they must love the smell of green."

Arbiter stops for a second and turns back to look at him.

"Or donations."

Chief turns his head to look at Johnson too.

"Or youkai having gay sex."

Behind them, Bisenti, Chips, and Mendoza's jaws drop, utterly astonished at the nonsense Chief was saying. Even Arby had gotten in on it, too. How did the Sarge not notice this?

Out of the bushes comes a third Elite, a Spec-Ops operator in navy blue power armor. His plasma rifle holstered to his thigh, he walks up to Arbiter with his hands clasped together. Interjecting the group's path, he lifts his hand up and shows the alien warrior something in his palm. Standing still calmly in his hand is a small frog.

"Look, Arbiter. I found this frog in a nearby creek. I think that it is very cute."

Arbiter examines the tiny animal closely, then looks back up at the Elite with the same hardened expression he's been wearing since the war started.

"By the rings, 'Sraom, you are right. This is indeed a very cute frog. I like snakes better, though."

Chief takes a look at the frog as well. 'Sraom lets him get close and look at it without hesitation.

"I think the little guy's pretty cool too. I love frogs and snakes equally."

Mission 2: Sierra 117

Rise up. Start the fight.

BGM: Released (from "Halo 3")

Walk It Off

It isn't long until the first actual battle of the game begins. Sanae, Kanako, and Suwako navigate through a narrow ravine path through the jungle while observing the beautiful bleeding edge game world from the point of view of the Master Chief and his new alien allies, complete with an immersive heads-up display simulating the actual insides of the super soldier's helmet. Stepping out of the pass and jumping over a rocky ledge, they are impeded by their first true enemies, a large ape-like alien commanding a huge group of short chimp-like ones.

"Okay, Moms, remember the combo! Just do what I told you to and we should be fine!" Sanae tells them.

The three of them take aim and open fire! The shrine becomes noisy with the rapid click of controllers, explosions, plasma blasts, and gunshots. Hot lead and plasma bolts streak all across the screen as the players and the ingame enemies exchange fire.

Suwako chews through the short aliens with the rapid fire of her character's plasma rifle, making quick work of alien after alien. Kanako shoots off the commander's shiny armor with her own rifle, causing it to shatter and fall off his body. Sanae aims the Master Chief's magnum at the big guy's newly-exposed head, and takes the shot. The blast instantly takes out the alien beast, and his cowardly subordinates flee for their lives.

"Got him!"

"Oh, they even flee in terror when their leaders die? This *really* takes me back..."

They take out the rest of the aliens with their guns and push forward through the jungle level. Each corner they pass reveals more and more alien invaders to slay. They deal with each one in a similar fashion to the first, with wild gunfire and well-placed headshots from Sanae. It never gets any less fun.

"Watch this!" Sanae says.

She grabs an alien's dropped gun, a strangely shaped plasma pistol. Approaching another big alien, she makes the Chief sidestep a grenade from it's launcher, charges a big blast on the pistol, and fires it back. It instantly blows all the armor off the alien soldier and makes him stagger back in pain. She switches weapons to the magnum and shoots it right in the head, killing it instantly. 

"Nice job, sweetie!" Kanako congratulates her.

"Thanks, Mom!" Sanae replies. "Now, trust me, don't do that to people in multiplayer or else they'll call you a fag!"

"Sanae, don't say that word around here, please." Suwako gently scolds her.

"Sorry, Mom..." she responds, remorsefully.

Walking up a tall cliff face, they are held back by a group of lizard-faced aliens standing side-by-side, hiding behind shields made of glowing energy held in one hand and firing plasma pistols in the other. They stay in an imposing phalanx formation, protected from opposing fire but able to lay down enough of their own to completely suppress the players and prevent passage.

"A shield wall? I've seen them plenty of times before." Kanako says. "But they've never been easier to deal with than this!"

Pressing down on the controller trigger makes Kanako's character throw a glowing blue ball of light at the alien formation. A plasma grenade! It lands at their feet, sticks to the ground, and makes a loud whine. A few of the enemy aliens notice it and make a vain attempt to dive to the side out of the way, while the rest cower in place. It explodes with a loud crackle of energy, sending blue plasma all around and blowing up all the aliens. Their bodies fly away and land on the ground like ragdolls.

"Ha, that was fun." Kanako says with a laugh.

"Didn't you say this game was stupidly hard on this difficulty?" Suwako asks Sanae.

"I think we just got lucky so far! The real bullshit should begin very soon..." Sanae answers ominously.

Charlie Foxtrot

Battling their way through every inch of forest, they approach the banks of a wide river, flanked by a white concrete pump station. Along the way, Sanae exchanges the Chief's magnum for a large scoped battle rifle she finds next to a deceased marine out of habit. Another familiar sight from previous games, she knows it will be essential for the rest of the game.

They fight through hordes of aliens, blowing them away with grenades and gunshots, until they reach the concrete platform around the pump station. Right as they arrive, three of the tall alien brutes ambush them from behind a large wooden crate, shooting a pummeling of bombs at them.

"Oh, no no no no! Nope, get back from them!" Sanae exclaims.

Sanae and Kanako navigate their characters behind a pillar, concealing themselves from danger for the moment. However, Suwako finds herself taken by suprise, and drops her controller! Her character takes the brunt of the grenades right in his split-lipped alien face. They explode and break through his protective energy shield, making the bar on top of the screen flash red and causing a constant beeping sound.

"Au au, I'm done for..." she mutters sheepishly.

Right before the beasts can fire again, Kanako throws a frag grenade at them from out of cover. It clatters to the ground in front of them, rolls to a stop, and then explodes. On Legendary difficulty, it only does enough damage to wreck their armor, but that's all Kanako needs. With their helmets knocked off by the explosion and the aliens left standing in a row, she circles around the concrete pillar, flanks them to the side, and shoots all three of them in the head, taking them all out at once! The whole complex trick brings a smile to her face.

"Ha ha ha, saved you, my little froggie!" she chuckles.

"Aw, maybe the snake really does have a big heart..." Suwako teases back, picking up her controller.

The three of them kill the rest of the alien troops and move on, the marines following behind them. The path takes them around the corner of the building and back into the jungle, where they pass by the trunks of huge trees.

Looking around, Sanae and her moms find no enemies around. In contrast to the huge battle they fought just to pass by the riverbank, this jungle was quiet. Far too quiet, her memories of Halo 2 told her. She looks up into the branches, scanning below the green canopies of the trees. Far too late, she notices the glints of many eyepieces, each belonging to numerous alien snipers perched on the thick tree branches and aiming beam rifles at them. She feels like they're staring out of the screen and into her very soul.

"Oh no! B-back up- ohhh!"

Her orders are interrupted by a whizzing noise from the game. A thin blue laser comes out of nowhere and cuts Master Chief's life short instantly, causing the screen to cut to a shot of his body falling limply to the ground. Sanae lets out a grunt of frustration.

"Huh?"

"What?"

The goddesses are taken by complete suprise. Two more whizzes from nowhere, and their characters are soundly beaten in an instant as well. The screen now shows all of their character's bodies laying still on the jungle floor. Sanae leans forward, stomping her feet and pouting in angered desperation.

"Fucking Jackal Snipers! Every single time! Ugh, this is gonna be a really hard game..."

Realizing how quickly it took for them to all be instantly pwned by the almighty Halo 3, Kanako and Suwako suddenly realize that they will most likely be going at this game all night. At least Sanae will be happy...

Disclaimer: You couldn't actually do three person splitscreen co-op in Halo 3 back in the Xbox 360 days. Back then, in the times of LAN parties, both consoles and PCs required you to either play over the Internet or connect multiple systems together using these nightmare cable setups if you wanted to play with a large group of friends. Obviously this is a moot point today because now everyone just plays against strangers in matchmaking, and Halo doesn't even have fucking splitscreen co-op anymore because of systemic corporate mismanagement. Thanks 343!

However, I'm omitting this detail here for the sake of brevity. Sanae should not have an entire story arc dedicated to setting up multiple consoles and television sets in her shrine, she should be playing Halo with her hot moms for this out of control gag tangent.

Fun fact: Suwako actually has the same "au au" catchphrase as Hanyuu from Higurashi. I feel like this might be an intentional reference. I've read an unsubstantiated rumor that before starting Higurashi, the writer wanted to make an official Touhou visual novel before ZUN turned him down and encouraged him to do something more creative on his own. I haven't seen a source for it, though. Still, an official Touhou visual novel written by Ryukishi07, based on the PC-98 games as well (as the first episode of Higurashi was released at the same time as EoSD during Comiket 62), would've literally changed history. Chapter 9: Stage 5: her name is big boobs look her up

Chapter Summary

The shrine maiden descends to the deepest recesses of Former Hell, an endless sea of madness and flame. In this sweltering nook of residual sin, only ancient vengeful spirits remain to play around the brimstone and lava plumes. Good thing she came here naked anyways! Will Reimu find Satori's shitty gay pets and uncover the cause of the haunted geysers down here, or will she be burned alive for her good intentions? How is she even alive in the first place?

...Was that a meow just now? Oh, fuck, don't tell me the damn cat is back for revenge...

Chapter Notes

See the end of the chapter for notes

Hellfires of Times Past

STAGE 5: Remains of the Blazing Hell

BGM: Lullaby of Deserted Hell

A wind hotter than any cock musk blows past Reimu's face. It blows her braids behind her head and rustles at her hair ribbon. Beads of sweat drop from her brow like raindrops, glowing a hot orange from the flame and brimstone below. Undeterred, Reimu continues flying forward into the endless flames without rest.

As soon as the piano notes in the stage theme start, a huge plume of lava erupts behind Reimu as high as a skyscraper! smoke, ash, and ember chokes out all the air that isn't on fire. Strong winds from the convection currents whip against her body, screaming into her ears. The fire and lava make her sweaty naked skin glimmer a bright orange-red.

More plumes of lava erupt up ahead like boiling roses. Constant, ear-pounding booms from the neverending tremors shake even the air itself, creating conditions that would drag even users of the most sophisticated flight magic down into a burning grave. None of this peril even startles Reimu. She flies through the fiery maelstrom like a kite on a calm, gently breezy day. Banking back and forth like she was following her whims for fun, she strafes past every single eruption of lava and fire like they aren't even dangerous at all.

The ying-yang crackles heavily, straining to convey Yukari's voice. It's hard for Reimu to make out the words from the static, especially with the roar of flame all around her.

"Reimu, the orb is almost out of energy. This is the last we'll be able to speak to you for a while." Yukari says, an uncharacteristic worry in her voice.

"What a relief. I've got my hands full with the flames and lava alone." Reimu responds dismissively.

"Human, you must be very careful. You could easily die down here if you don't pay attention." Yukari continues. "These flames are more dangerous than even most of the youkai you've fought. I'd hate to lose you."

"Yukari's right. I'd hate to have to write an article about your agonizing death, human." Aya adds. "Whatever happens, make sure you make it back up to us in one piece! Gensokyo needs you, ayayaya!"

"Gahahaha- *hic*! Don't 'sweat' it, Reimu! You're more than tough enough to kick ol' Hell's ass. Just charge the orb by punchin' the mastermind's shit in, and we'll be back before you can say "sake"!" Suika encourages her. "Whatever ya do, don't give up now!"

As annoyed as the shrine maiden was at each of them, in her heart she could tell each of the youkai truly cared about her. Not even for selfish reasons. For the first time in a while, she felt the need to reciprocate that warmth back.

"I... I will. Nothing down here is going to kill me." she says into the orb. "And everyone? This doesn't pay any of you back for using my shrine as a playground, but... thank you for helping me. I'll be sure to put an end to this incident, whatever it is."

"Reimu, no, thank y... *skhhhhh*..."

Before Yukari can finish, the noise from the orb fizzles out and goes silent. Not wanting to betray the final words of her friends, Reimu continues into the sea of fire.

The Remains of Burning Hell truly was vast. For a tiny portion of Hell still not extinguished, there seemed like endless fire and lava to fly around. No matter how far she went, only more flame and ash rose to greet her. Occasionally vengeful spirits would pop out of the lava and explode into danmaku, but she would dodge their shots easily. Besides, you helped us meet our youkai exterminating quota for this incident! Now, show us where your friend is hiding, and we'll put a stop to this incident once and for all."

Orin's ears perk up, and she grins again.

"Oh, of course! I, like, came to ya here because ya took the wrong path. This place's a dead end! The bird ya gotta deal with is back the other way. And also, I know we just fought, but ya can't pick a fight with her when we go to stop her! I'm being serious, it's reeeeally important, nya! She's been ranting about nuking the ENTIRE surface world, and I'm positive she's able to do it! If she tries to fight someone with all that power, it'll be really dangerous for everyone 'cuz she can't control it! Ya gotta fuck the crazy outta her, without fighting, before the oni hear about it and get us in trouble! I repeat, don't fight her, nya!"

Reimu stands up, giving Orin a nod.

"So just fucking? Whatever you say, if it stops Gensokyo from getting nuked."

The youkai cat stands up beside her.

"Thanks for understanding, nya! Now, if only your bestie in the big hat was here so I could warn her, too. Where is she?"

"Oh, Marisa? We split up at the fork in the giant maze of huge flames so we could both search faster. I went this way, and she went the other way."

Orin's eyes widen with worry, and her tails curl together.

"The other way? She's, like, right down that way! Your friend won't go all out in a fight, would she? Hopefully not, nya!"

Reimu exhales sarcastically.

"Nope, Marisa absolutely would go all out and fight her. There's no chance she would ever hold back, even if you told her."

Orin gasps with fear, and her tails stick straight up.

"Oh SHIT, NYA! That's bad, really bad! Listen to me, if they both go at eachother at full strength, they'll destroy EVERYTHING!"

Chapter End Notes

This is one of my favorite stages conceptually. Flying through just straight up fire in Hell is a very shmup-style concept, which is even more fitting for the upcoming final boss. It kinds stands out, but then you remember that the guy comes up with awesome stage concepts like "endless floating door dimension", the Dream World, Makai, the Netherworld stairs and Miko's mausoleum thing literally every game. They might not be the most fleshed out in writing but they're extremely striking visually. Stuff that isn't le generic outside area is extremely good.

I gotta confess I have never beaten Orin. I usually die to her first or second spell card even on easy. So, consider this to be revenge.

We're almost at the end of Touhou 11's story. One more peek at our heroic group of gamers and their valiant efforts to destroy Israel (by yelling at things on a screen) and we will finally confront everyone's favorite big bird with big boobs and get cancer.

I kind of wish we were on Touhou 12 already so I can get it finished before it's too late. The USA is already getting attacked by UFOs or something so in a little while it's going to be seen as distasteful and offensive to write porn of an alien thing like Nue. Brandon is gonna take away our nuenis...

Also, thanks for 28 kudos and 2000+ hits! This series is nothing without the endless support you guys give me. As usual, feel free to give me your feedback and suggestions in the comments! Chapter 10: Intermission V: yeah they do the warthog run in this one

Chapter Summary

yep, they're doing it

Chapter Notes

See the end of the chapter for notes

Intermission V

Mission 10: Halo

Light the Ring. Destroy the Flood.

BGM: Halo Reborn (from "Halo 3")

Sanae and her parents stayed up all night playing Halo 3, from start to finish, in a single sitting. With divinity running through their veins, none of them took a single break. They were glued to the edges of their seats, hooked by the game's next generation action and mystery. Not a single one of them wanted to stop playing.

As unbelievable as it may be, they somehow managed to beat the game on the Legendary difficulty without any prior experience, all over the course of a single night. They managed to save Earth from the alien invaders, traveled through a portal to a mysterious disc world known as "The Ark", defeated the Covenant there for good by killing the treacherous Prophet of Truth, and saved the AI construct Cortana from capture by the despicable parasitic Flood zombies.

Now, their final mission was to go back to where it all started; land on an incomplete recreation of the first game's Halo Ring, fire the life-destroying superweapon in an ironic twist of fate, and destroy the Ring, the Arc, and the last of the Flood. After this task, the galaxy would surely be at peace at last, and Master Chief's journey to save humanity would finally end. There surely wouldn't be any shitty reboot games, or something, after this.

On the screen, the Master Chief and his big alien friend (they were chill with eachother now) crash land in a snowy valley. They were close to Halo's control room, and simply needed to get there, activate the ring, and escape before the whole thing blew up.

"This is it, guys. This is the last level!" Sanae exclaims excitedly.

Switching back to first person, the three of them walk the heroes through the desolate valley. Despite them all being armed to the teeth, the path was suprisingly empty for a final level. 

"Where are all the monsters?" Suwako asks.

"Most likely hiding up ahead to build up the tension." Kanako explains. "If the rest of this game is any indication, the final level shall be no easy victory."

They walk beneath an overpass concealing a bit of a submerged metal structure. Then, the valley opens up into a large snowy field surrounded on all sides by cliff faces. On the other side is a large metal ziggurat with a huge door on the top. Sanae recognizes it almost immediately.

"Dammit, they're making me play through Assault on the Control Room AGAIN!!!"

They trek across the field and head up the metal ziggurat, trading the crunch of snow underfoot with the clank of metal. Every step of the way, they are constantly attacked by an endless rain of Flood zombies falling from the sky towards them. They die many times and have to start over at the last checkpoint, but eventually reach the very top. Once there, they fend off the rest of the zombies until the massive doors open then head inside.

Within is the Halo ring's temple-like control room, where the team reunites with Sgt. Johnson and activates the unfinished ring. However, for attempting to destroy Halo, they are attacked by a floating metal orb shikigami still loyal to his long-gone masters. It kills Sgt. Johnson by shooting him in the chest with a giant red laser beam!

"Nooo! They killed Seargent Johnson!" Sanae gasps in horror. "He was one of my favorite guys in the game!"

A single tear rolls down Sanae's cheek and drips down onto the collar of her pajamas when the reality hits her. She wasn't about to mourn a fictional character from a goofy video game. Johnson's death was just that moving to her. Despite him not being real, he was like a genuine bro to her who had battled by Master Chief's, and by extension her very own, side since she played the first game all those years ago. Even a woman like her could deeply understand the reassuring fraternity his presence brought to the alien worlds she explored through the Master Chief's eyes. With Johnson's death, the series would not be able to continue in his absence. The meaning was clear. This was the end.

So that's why, when she takes the dying man's laser gun, she blasts apart the metal shikigami without mercy.

As Chief finally sabotages the ring, and says his silent goodbyes to his comrade, her chest is pumping full of all sorts of emotions. Grief, anger, relief, fear. Johnson's final words hone them all into a sharp spear, aimed straight at one single target and ready to be thrown with purpose.

"Send me out. With a bang..."

The trio of gamers make their way out of the control room as the massive Halo ring shakes itself to pieces all around them. They make their way onto a snowy cliffside, battling zombies and angry flying robots dead set on avenging the destruction of their ring. They reach a metal tunnel dug into the cliffs, which leads them into a room Sanae immediately recognizes as being copied directly from the first game. Cursing the lazy game developers with every curse they could inflict on them, they cut a swath through the crowded rooms and come out onto another path outside. There, they find a parked jeep with a mounted machine gun, which Cortana remarks must've been driven here by the late Johnson. This was their ticket to the space frigate off this ring.

"Oh, a Warthog! Everyone, get in!" Sanae tells them.

"Let me use the minigun this time, dear!" Suwako asks.

"Sure thing, honey. I'll get in the passenger seat, then." Kanako says.

Sanae's character climbs into the driver's seat, and everyone else gets into the spot they agreed on. Tilting the joystick on the controller, Sanae makes the car accelerate forward and steers it through the snowy pass. It rolls around a turn on a dime, carrying all three of them at once.

It doesn't take them long to leave the rocky path. What lies beyond is... nothing. They've been led to a section of the ring that was unfinished, and would remain that way forever. In place of rocks, trees, and nature, there were vast stretches of metal platforms and ramps. Exploding metal platforms and ramps. Everything was being torn apart by Halo's firing sequence, sending sheets of metal the size of houses flying around them like dropped toys. Realistic physics on this scale was a magical feat for a video game like this, so the presentation awed all of them. What awed Sanae even more was when a familiar set of drums started banging.

BGM: Greatest Journey (from "Halo 3")

"It's the... the Warthog Run! I can't believe it! They brought it back from the first game!"

There's no other path to the end of the level besides straight through this dangerous maze of exploding metal. The perfect ending for Halo 3, of course, so nobody playing would've had it any other way. Sanae drives the jeep off of the path onto the metal sheets, flanked on both sides by explosions and plumes of flame. As soon as they set off, the plates start exploding behind them! The excitement changes the Moriya Shrine into a den of cheering and hollering.

"Go, Sanae, go!"

Watch out!"

Metal platforms explode on the path up ahead, leaving deadly pitfalls in their place. For every one Sanae steers around, dozens more appear further on. No matter how many obstacles this game threw at her, she was determined to overcome them all. It also helped that she was having the time of her life!

"Yeah! I knew this game would be awesome! This one's even better than the one in the first game!"

"Don't lose focus, honey! Keep driving!"

They drive off a ramp and sail through the air, landing inside a large metal structure with a path that curved around walls. Without even letting go of the gas, Sanae continues driving the car forward as soon as the wheels hit the ground with a loud clank. Their path is obstructed by groups of zombies and robots fighting eachother! They ignore the Chief and his passengers, but their lasers and bullets still streak back and forth across the pathway like a spell card barrage. There was no time to hit the brakes, as the entire platform was already leaning to the side and ready to fall over!

"Sanae, dear, I'll handle this!" Suwako orders the human. "Just keep driving, and don't stop!"

Suwako takes aim at the group of robots with the machine gun and fires away. The barrels spin and spin, giving off steam from the heat of the rounds, and a waterfall of brass casings cascades out of the side of the gun. The flock of flying robots get hit by the bullets and explode into metal scrap and plasma, like exterminated fairies from the future.

The zombies turn their attention to Sanae now, but far too late. Before they can do their pounce attack, Sanae runs them over in the car at full speed! Most of the zombies get blown apart into diseased limbs and chunks of flesh with a spooky scream. The car accelerates off of the structure and lands back on the sea of exploding platforms with a tiny bounce before zooming forward again.

Suwako fires the machine gun at every foe in sight, not letting go of the trigger even once. Kanako backs her up, firing away with the Plasma Rifle the Arbiter she controlled held from the passenger seat. Sanae puts her faith in her gods and focuses solely on driving through the treacherous metal path without tipping the car over or falling into the abyss below. The two gods shout out warnings about enemies or suprise obstacles, which she drives around every time.

"Keep shooting, you two!"

"Sanae, watch out for that guy!"

They drive into a massive tunnel filled with more warring monsters. The path is a shattered mess of ramps and platforms of varying heights. As Sanae drives forward, a huge metal girder starts to twist and fall from above. She drives past right before it hits and barrels through another group of zombies before they can attack her.

"Sanae, look! A secret passage!" Kanako says, pointing right in front of them on the screen.

Right in front of them was a long metal beam running beneath the path of platforms above. It was a shortcut that would lead them past the maze of ramps and enemies.

"I'm on it, Lady Kanako!" Sanae replies, driving right on top of the beam. She follows it all the way to the end, steering herself straight constantly to avoid slipping off but still not slowing down. The end of the beam is slanted into a ramp. She drives them off of it, and the car sails through the air! A huge pillar of fire erupts right in front of them, which they shoot through with a resounding chorus of gasps. The car lands back on more metal platforms outside the tunnel and Sanae keeps driving forward.

As they drive on, the destruction gets even more fierce. They head out of another tunnel, and see the escape spaceship parked in the distance up ahead! Huge metal pillars around them start tipping over and crashing into the path, biting chunks out of it like a hungry ghost princess. One pillar blows up the panels in front of them, sending them flying right towards the screen! Sanae even flinches like it was real.

"This is getting insane! I- I think i's almost over! Just keep shooting, and I'll get us through this!"

The ship was around a half-finished mountain range, a huge unsightly mound of rock nearly a mile wide that the crumbling platforms led around. They would have to drive around this if they were to escape.

The explosions start to catch up to, and even overcome them. Entire yards of metal platform, some as huge as the shrine grounds, get blown away by explosion after explosion. Only narrow stretches of plate remain for them to drive over. Thinking quickly, Sanae steers back to safety as the panels blow up to avoid driving them all off the edge. She just barely makes it past each one.

They take a turn past the rock, and see an impossibly large metal pillar fall by the wayside. It takes more than half of the path with it into oblivion as it swipes by. Just a narrow stretch of path is left. Sanae steers right, hard, to avoid careening off the edge. She reacted just in time to avoid sending the jeep right off as it turned.

"There! Look, everyone!"

"Perfect!"

"Just a little more! Step on it, dear!"

With the last turn, the ship finally comes into view! It floats in the sky right beyond the edge of a long stretch of platforms. Sanae drives towards it as fast as she can, steering past more holes and explosions than ever before. They're so close, they can see right into the ship's open cargo bay hatch. At the very end of the path was a ramp, which would hopefully let them jump right into the ship. Or, it should, right? It was their only chance. Sanae aligns the car straight on with the open hatch, and drives toward the ramp. As the end approaches, she takes a deep breath and holds it.

Chief assesses the distance between the ramp and the Forward Unto Dawn's rear cargo bay. If they drove off at full speed, they possibly could make it. Or, more likely, they would miss and fall into the depths of the self-destructing Halo, where they would be torn apart by the ring's gravity well if they didn't manage to land on debris after a mile-long fall. That is, if the ring itself didn't kill them first. This was most likely the most perilous, amazing stunt to ever be performed by someone in the UNSC for all of time. It would take a miracle to actually pull it off.

The edge approaches. Master Chief never once lifted his feet off the gas pedal of the Warthog, so it was going full speed, pedal fully pressed into the floor, the whole time. Cortana's voice speaks to Chief through his neural implant.

"Gun it, Chief! Jump!" she exclaims in great panic.

"I promised you before, Cortana. We will make it." he tells her calmly.

"I am not entirely sure about that, Demon. This jump may well be the end of us all." Arbiter says.

"We'll make it. We all put our faith in eachother. Just believe in me." Chief says back to him.

His words seem strangely convincing to all of them. Even N'tho, perched precariously to the back of the Warthog's turret, raised no further complaints. Chief straightens the Warthog's bearing one last time, then drives it straight off the ramp. It whooshes high into the air in a beautiful arc, like it was a Banshee instead. The ring's mysterious mechanisms shake the air itself around them with terrifying booms. The last of the ground behind them explodes.

The cargo bay of the Autumn is in sight. Just a few feet away from the front wheels! The Warthog starts to descend from the air, right towards the ship's open hatch. As fast as it seemed they would be saved, the Warthog suddenly starts to fall *too* fast. At this trajectory, they would miss the hatch and fall. They were doomed!

Master Chief lifts his hand off the steering wheel. In his hand, he holds a crumpled card. It looked more like a wrapper in his oversized glove. He holds it up, and it starts to glow.

Miracle "Blow Me Away"

A terrible updraft of wind gusts up from below the Warthog and blows it back upward! It is strong enough to lift the vehicle and its passengers back towards the Dawn's cargo bay. It flies right in, flipping over and sliding across the floor with a loud screech and a trail of sparks, until it crashes into the far wall.

Miraculously, the trio emerge from the crash unharmed. They were not destined to die here. They still needed to pilot the ship away from Halo, and escape! The ship suddenly tips to the side, slightly. A huge Scorpion tank starts to slide across the cargo bay, right towards Arbiter and N'tho! The two Elites immediately make a run for it towards the exit, with the Scorpion following behind them. Right as they get through, the Scorpion slams into the wall, sending down heavy metal crates that block the exit.

Chief runs over to check if they made it okay. Arbiter widens a gap between two boxes in the heap, and nods at him through it. Chief nods back, understanding immediately. There was no time for words now. Only action.

Chief sprints over to a computer terminal, data chip in hand, and plugs Cortana into it. The familiar blue hologram of a blue naked woman comes out of a projector on top, and speaks to him.

"Hold on!" she shouts.

The Dawn's engines fire up, and the ship starts to lift off from the ring. It turns up and flies straight upward into the sky! The cargo bay becomes a downward ramp, prompting Chief to clutch onto the terminal for dear life. Cargo boxes start to fall out of the ship all around him.

Chief is left dangling from the computer, with the molten red skeleton of Halo far below him. The cargo bay is filled with a loud screech as the Warthog they rode in on starts to slide towards him. The ship flies perfectly vertically, and the Warthog suddenly falls straight down. The bumper hits Chief in the shoulder as it passes by, knocking him away from the computer into a free fall!

The Chief tumbles through the air helplessly towards the cargo hatch. He manages to press himself up against the floor, desperately clambering for a handhold as he slides towards certain demise. His hand slides over a series of metal grooves in the floor, which had become a ladder at this angle. Just before he falls out of the ship, he jams his hand straight into the groove and holds on, stopping his fall!

"Chief!" Cortana calls out after him.

Chief hears a loud banging above him. Looking straight up, he sees the massive Scorpion tank falling straight towards him! He cowers his head down towards the wall right before it hits him. The Scorpion flies down past him, barely missing decapitating him with it's tread, and falls out of the cargo bay towards the Halo ring. With the coast clear, Chief starts climbing up the floor grooves back up towards Cortana.

On top of the computer, Cortana falls to her knees with worry for Chief, holding her hand out to him like he could actually grab it. Right as Halo starts to fire, Chief makes back up to her, and rises up between her and the ringworld's glare.

In space, the ship's gravity systems stabilize the cargo bay, keeping everything firmly on the ground again. Arbiter reaches the ship's bridge and hops in the captain's seat, then charts a course right into the portal back to Earth. Back in the cargo bay Chief sits behind the computer console and plugs Cortana back into his helmet, protecting them from the incoming blast.

"If we don't make it..." Cortana starts.

"We'll make it. I didn't use any continues." Chief interrupts her.

"It's been an honor serving with you, John... Wait, what did you say?" Cortana tells him, before realizing what the Chief had just said. "Continues? Chief, what are you talking about-"

Chief rests his head against the computer console in silence. The entire cargo bay is flooded with a blinding flash of white light.

BGM: Never Forget (from "Halo 3")

After the climactic finale of the last level, the game plays its final cutscene. The surviving humans rescue Arbiter from the front half of the ship, which had made it back to Earth and crashed into the ocean. Afterwards, they hold a memorial ceremony on a hill dedicated to the lives lost in the war. The admiral of the marine forces gives a speech honoring everyone lost defending mankind, before thanking the Arbiter for helping the Chief at the very end.

"Hard to believe he's dead."

"Were it so easy."

The alien returns to his own spaceship, and reunites with its shipmaster at the helm. They talk about the hope they have for their own futures now that they aren't indoctrinated by the Covenant's lies about Halo anymore. After gathering the rest of the aliens on board, they fly off and head back to their homeworld.

The game cuts to the final scene aboard the back half of the ship, where Master Chief and Cortana were left behind when the portal closed in front of them. It drifts aimlessly in the bright blue nebula of deep space, sliced in half down the middle as if by a hot blade.

The Chief floats down a dark metal hallway in the ship, almost like how Sanae herself flew around in the air. He goes up to another projector in the cryotube bay, where Cortana pops out and tells him what happened.

"But you did it." she continues. "Truth and the Covenant, the Flood... It's finished."

"It's finished." he repeats with a nod.

The man floats over to a cryo pod against the wall. He pulls out his assault rifle and clicks it into a rack beside it, then opens up the pod. Cortana says she'll send out a distress beacon from the ship. It might take several years for them to be rescued, if at all. In the meantime, all Chief could do is rest.

"I'll miss you." she says to him as he gets inside the pod and closes the door.

The pod door closes around Chief like a coffin. He looks just like he did in the very first game, where he emerged from an identical-looking one to fight off the aliens on the very first ringworld. Right before the lid closes, he offers Cortana one last goodbye.

"Wake me... when you need me."

Sanae gently puts the controller down on the floor by her feet. Her knuckles were pure white. That truly was the greatest video game she'd ever play, no doubt about it. And even better, she got to experience it with her family, two of the people she loved the most in all of Gensokyo.

Of course, her parents. The end of the game jogs her memory. She had them play this game for a reason. There was something important she had to do. With the Chief finally retired from his work, she had to step up and be the hero now. And the first thing she would save was her own family.

She stands up and walks over to Suwako.

"See, Lady Suwako? Look! Did you notice how all the people in the game believed Master Chief would save them from the aliens? Even though they live in a high-tech world run by science, they still had faith Master Chief could do the impossible, no matter how dangerous things got! He had luck as his superpower, and it was more important to him than his suit of armor or his gun! Even in a world run by science, faith can coexist!"

Suwako looks up at her, confused.

"But... isn't it just a story, Sanae? How do you know that faith works like that in real life?"

Sanae puts her hand on Suwako's shoulder.

"Because, I went to school and learned about science, remember? The people in the story are just like real ones! Trust me, the more you learn about science, the less you truly understand the world. Each breakthrough opens up tons of more mysteries for us to solve. The deeper you get, the harder it is to find more answers! For example, there isn't even a unified theory that explains how gravity works in relation with the rest of physics! Eventually, it becomes seemingly impossible us to progress further. At that point, science is about just believing in theories and frameworks without reason, not exactly knowing why things work that way. Isn't that just faith?"

Tears well up in Suwako's eyes. She stands up and shakes Sanae's hand.

"I... think I understand, now. Thank you for clearing things up, Sanae. I feel a lot better now about Kanako's new business model. I was just so... worried, before, about our safety. I never wanted to hurt anyone."

Sanae gives her a smile back and straightens out her big frog hat.

"I figured that, Lady Suwako. I won't ever hold it against you. Just don't be scared of science as a god, okay?"

She turns over to Kanako, who was also standing up next to her.

"And Lady Kanako, you should've learned something from the game too! Remember how the aliens lied about the rings in order to push their phony religion? They used the faith the other aliens had in them to coerce them into doing bad things, like taking over the galaxy and trying to destroy all the humans! And in the end, the alien prophet guy got killed by his former follower for what he did. Lady Kanako, I think we should stop using faith like they did and be more honest in how our shrine operates! No more schemes that involve tricking people in order to gather faith. We should learn to coexist normally with the Hakurei Shrine, the youkai, and everyone else who lives in Gensokyo! There's more than enough faith to go around for everyone."

Kanako looks at her, just as confused as her wife was.

"You... think my plans are like the evil genocidal aliens from your video game, Sanae?"

Sanae shakes her head.

"No! Well, kinda, but not really! It's just not good to run our shrine this way. It makes a lot of people angry, and it could all fall apart in a day if someone decides they've had enough! I'd like us to make real friends in Gensokyo, not just business partners and gullible worshippers! Me and Lady Suwako care about you, and we know deep down you aren't an evil person. I just want you to not end up that way, like the aliens Master Chief had to beat to save humanity!"

Kanako hangs her head. Swallowing her pride, she responds to Sanae.

"I... understand now. I've been doing this for so long, I forgot about how much I love Suwako and you. I see now that it doesn't have to be like this. Thank you, Sanae, for showing me your game. From now on, I'll be a benevolent god sponsoring science who gathers faith by helping people. Profit won't be my highest priority anymore. I'm sorry for making all of you worry."

Sanae steps aside and directs Kanako and Suwako to face eachother.

"Don't just say it to me, you two, say it to eachother! Make up and stop fighting so we can be a happy family again!"

Kanako and Suwako step close and look deep into eachother's eyes, holding eachother's hands.

"I forgive your arrogance, my ambitious little snake." Suwako says to Kanako.

"I forgive your mistrust, too, my timid little frog." she says back to her.

The two hug eachother, wrapping their arms around eachother's shoulders and pulling them close. Kanako rests her chin on top of Suwako's hat, in between the two eyeballs. Then, they both turn over to Sanae.

"Thank you, Sanae!" they say in unison, hugging her too.

"Don't thank me, you two." Sanae replies, blushing. "Thank Master Chief."

They both chuckle. Kanako rubs the top of Sanae's hair.

"No, Master Chief isn't real. It was all thanks to you. I think you're tired from staying up late, honey. Go to bed, and we will let you sleep in late tomorrow morning. Now, me and your mother have some hot goddess sex we must catch up on. Right, honey~?"

Suwako opens her mouth, and her long frog tongue shoots out and touches Kanako's busts.

"Yesh, ehehehe~!"

Sanae pouts and crosses her arms, looking up at them.

"B-but I wanna join too! I let you two play my video game, and stuff!"

Kanako shakes her head.

"Not in this state, honey! You're too tired to have an orgy with two gods. You can join us tommorrow when you wake up."

Sanae sighs, disappointed.

"But I can... *yaaaawn*..."

Sanae's eyes close, and she leans forward, half asleep, against the two goddesses. They embrace her lovingly again, carefully brushing at her hair and caressing her cheek. She looked so cute like this, they both thought. The two of them stay there, hugging eachother and Sanae, while the television shows Master Chief's derelict spaceship floating close to a massive metal planet.

Chapter 11: Stage 6: Legalize Nuclear Birds

Chapter Summary

Marisa and her partners manage to finally track down the person behind the geysers within the most unlikely location imaginable: a nuclear fission power plant in the remains of Hell! The culprit turns out to be a bird-brained youkai with an awesome cape, big wings, an arm cannon, and big boobs! She seems to have gone mad with the power of nuclear fission itself, though, and now seeks to incinerate the ENTIRE surface of the Earth with nuclear hellfire!

Will Marisa emerge from the flames of Hell alive? Will she she even be able to get close enough to this crazy triple-legged bird to fuck her without being incinerated into ashes? Oh fuck, did we really trust the fate of the entire world to a perverted drug addict magician with a rocket launcher?

Chapter Notes

See the end of the chapter for notes

The Tempestuous Second Sun

STAGE 6: The Deepest Part of the Underground City

BGM: Hellfire Mantle

The pipes running along the walls of the nuclear reactor control center burst open, sending out blasts of hot steam. Rows of computer screens flash red before cracking and bursting into sparks and showers of glass. The wail of klaxon alarms scream out from all directions, bouncing off the metal walls, loud enough to give one a splitting headache.
